这个法规的颁布，犹如给我们配备了上方宝剑。

be too familiar with each other to stand on ceremony
拘泥于形式
jūnì yú xíngshì
rigidly adhere to form; be formalistic
拘泥于细节
jūnì yú xìjié
be very punctilious
拘泥成说
jūnì chéngshuō
rigidly adhere to accepted theories
拘守成规
jūshǒu chénɡɡuī
hold fast to convention
拘守绳墨
jūshǒu shéngmò
stick to the rules
不要拘束孩子们的正当活动。
Búyào jūshù háizimen de zhèngdànghuódòng。
Don\'t restrict the proper activities of children.
在生人面前显得拘束
zài shēngrén miànqián xiǎnde jūshù
look ill at ease in the presence of strangers
不要拘束。
Búyào jūshù。
Make yourself at home.
拘役的期限为十五日以上，六个月以下。
Jūyì de qīxiàn wéi shíwǔ rì yǐ shàng，liù gè yuè yǐ xià。
The term of criminal detention is not less than fifteen days and not more than six months.
在无拘无束的气氛中
zài wújūwúshù de qìfēn zhōng 
in an unconstrained atmosphere

Dàjiā wújūwúshù de fābiǎo yìjiàn。
Everyone expressed his views freely.
不拘形迹
bù jū xínɡjì
without formality; not standing on ceremony
把拘留犯移送市政法机关
bǎ jūliúfàn yísòng shìzhèngfǎjīguān

拘谨
jūjǐn
overcautious; reserved
拘泥
jūnì

拘束
jūshù
restrain; restrict
拘押
jūyā
take into custody; detain

恳求某物
Though her voice was toneless, it plead more loudly than words.
虽然她的声音听起来很沉闷，但是其中的恳求之意比言语更有力。
He begged her to stop cheating on him.
Tā kěnqiú tā búyào zài qīpiàn tā le。
他恳求她不要再欺骗他了。
He begged me to go myself to break the news to her.
Tā kěnqiú wǒ dúzì líkāi，qù bǎ zhège xiāoxi gàosu tā。
他恳求我独自离开，去把这个消息告诉她。
Management pleaded with workers not to strike.
Guǎnlǐcéng kěnqiú gōngrénmen búyào bàgōng。
管理层恳求工人们不要罢工。
The manager pleaded with his employees to keep about their duties while on he went on vacation.

经理恳求他的员工在他度假期间继续履行他们的职责。
No amount of pleading would allow them to let us through.

再多的恳求还是不能叫他们允许我们通过。

Wǒmen jiāng huì chéngkěn de tǎolùn shēnghuó de xiànshí。
我们将会诚恳地讨论生活的现实。

我恳求医生对我的病人进行移植手术。
The prophet bid all people to become good persons.

先知恳求所有的人都变成好人。

Hēnglì Sìshì kěnqiú jiàohuáng tóngyì tā líhūn。

Wǒ kěnqiú tā tíng xiàlái。
我恳求他停下来。

“Nǐ bìxū bāng wǒ，”tā kěnqiú de shuō。

He supplicated the king for clemency.
Tā kěnqiú guówáng kāi\'ēn。
他恳求国王开恩。
I importune you to help them.
Wǒ kěnqiú nǐ qù bāngzhù tāmen。
我恳求你去帮助他们。
态度诚恳
tàidu chéngkěn 
be sincere in what one does and says
诚恳地接受别人的意见
chéngkěn de jiēshòu biérén de yìjiàn 
listen to other people\'s criticisms with an open mind
待人诚恳
dàirén chéngkěn 
treat people sincerely; be sincere with people
诚恳悔过
chéngkěn huǐguò 
sincerely repent one\'s error; show sincere repentance

撒谎
sāhuǎng
tell a lie; lie
圆谎
yuánhuǎng
patch up a lie
我们一定要揭露出被谎言包囊的事实。
Wǒmen yídìng yào jiēlòuchū bèi huǎngyán bāonáng de shìshí。
We are determined to reveal facts that have been hidden by lies.
这个犯罪嫌疑人没有通过测谎仪的测试。
Zhège fànzuì xiányírén méiyǒu tōngguò cèhuǎngyí de cèshì。
The suspect didn\'t pass the lie detector test.
商贩经常报谎价以便获得更高的利润。
Shāngfàn jīngcháng bào huǎngjià yǐbiàn huòdé gènggāo de lìrùn。
Peddleries usually overbid to gain more profits.
他带来的消息不属实，是谎信。
Tā dàilái de xiāoxi bùshǔshí，shì huǎngxìn。
The news he purchased wasn\'t true, he had purchased false information.
他的谎言被我揭破了，但他却一点也不羞愧。

I exposed his lies, but he seemed not be ashamed at all.
被戳穿谎言之后，他的脸部表情异常地不自然。

When his lies were exposed, his expression was very unnatural.
他用这个弥天大谎诈骗了上亿元资金。

He has defrauded billions in capital by telling a real whopper.
他肯定是在说谎，前后说的话自相矛盾。
Tā kěndìng shì zài shuōhuǎng，qiánhòu shuō de huà zìxiāng máodùn。
He must be lying, because what he said is self-contradictory.
我从来不对别人撒谎。
Wǒ cónglái búduì biérén sāhuǎng。
I have never told a lie to anyone.
他没有通过测谎仪的检验，被判有罪。
Tā méiyǒu tōngguò cèhuǎngyí de jiǎnyàn，bèi pàn yǒuzuì。
编造谎言
biānzào huǎngyán
invent a lie
